# Claude.ai Session Guide — Ahmedabad 2026

> 129 attendees · April 2026 · Ahmedabad
> No terminal needed — everything works in your browser at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai)

> 💡 **All tools below are clickable links** — click any tool name to go directly to its website. No technical knowledge required.

## Per-Attendee Analysis

---

### Amish Thaker — Startup Founder
**Burning Problem:** Sales outbound at scale
**Building:** Not specified

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- connect-apps (Composio) — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — connects [Gmail](https://mail.google.com)/[LinkedIn](https://linkedin.com)/CRM for outbound sequences
- content-research-writer — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — researches prospects, drafts personalized cold outreach
- subagent-driven-development — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — spawn parallel agents per prospect segment
- Ruflo — Use **Projects** in [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) (left sidebar → New Project) for organized AI workspaces — orchestrate multi-step outbound pipeline (research → draft → send → follow-up)
- Caveman — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — keep token burn low on large prospect lists

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **Deep Research** — In [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) chat, click "Deep Research" to have Claude research the web for you — live prospect research before outreach
- **[Slack](https://slack.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Slack](https://slack.com) → Connect — push outbound summaries to sales channel

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Draft 10 personalized cold emails for [ICP description]. Research each company with brave-search, extract pain points, write 3-line subject + 5-line body. Output as CSV with name,email,subject,body columns.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Amish — Outbound Sales Automation
- Stack: Gmail, LinkedIn, CRM (specify), CSV exports
- Focus: Personalized cold outreach at scale, follow-up sequences
- Style: Terse output, sales-focused tone, no fluff
```

### Parth Jala — Startup Founder
**Burning Problem:** Client outreach, onboarding, funnel creation
**Building:** Not specified

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- connect-apps (Composio) — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — automate funnel touchpoints across email/[Slack](https://slack.com)/[Notion](https://notion.so)
- subagent-driven-development — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — separate agents for outreach vs onboarding vs nurture
- Ruflo — Use **Projects** in [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) (left sidebar → New Project) for organized AI workspaces — stitch full funnel pipeline as orchestrated workflow
- content-research-writer — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — generate onboarding docs and welcome sequences

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Notion](https://notion.so)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Notion](https://notion.so) → Connect — write onboarding SOPs and client docs directly
- **[Slack](https://slack.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Slack](https://slack.com) → Connect — automate client welcome messages
- **[Google Drive](https://drive.google.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Google Drive](https://drive.google.com) → Connect — store and version onboarding materials

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Build onboarding checklist for new client [name]. Pull from Notion template, generate welcome email, create Slack welcome message, output 30-day milestone tracker.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Parth — Client Funnel Automation
- Stack: Notion, Slack, Email (specify CRM)
- Focus: Outreach → onboard → nurture funnel
- Style: Structured outputs, milestone-driven
```

### Prakruti Joshi — Business Owner/Freelancer
**Burning Problem:** Work smarter — reduce manual effort across freelance ops
**Building:** Not specified

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- Caveman — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — token-efficient for daily task batching
- connect-apps (Composio) — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — link [Gmail](https://mail.google.com), calendar, invoicing tools
- content-research-writer — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — proposals, reports, client comms
- Everything Claude Code (ECC) — Available via [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills — full workflow harness

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **File Upload** — In any [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) chat, click the paperclip icon to upload Excel, PDF, Word, or CSV files — read/write local docs and templates
- **[Google Drive](https://drive.google.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Google Drive](https://drive.google.com) → Connect — manage client deliverables

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Review my week's emails (paste 5 threads). Summarize action items per client, draft replies, flag anything urgent. Output: per-client action list + draft replies.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Prakruti — Freelance Ops
- Stack: Gmail, Google Drive, local files
- Focus: Reduce repeat manual tasks, faster client communication
- Style: Bullet outputs, direct tone
```

- changelog-generator — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — track ops process changes over time

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Notion](https://notion.so)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Notion](https://notion.so) → Connect — SOPs, process docs, runbooks
- **File Upload** — In any [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) chat, click the paperclip icon to upload Excel, PDF, Word, or CSV files — local ops data access

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Map my current ops workflow: [describe process]. Identify 3 bottlenecks. Suggest automation for each. Output: bottleneck + current effort + automation solution + tool needed.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Devesh — Business Operations

- Style: Process-oriented, structured tables
```

- **[Google Drive](https://drive.google.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Google Drive](https://drive.google.com) → Connect — store content calendar and drafts

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Topic: [your niche]. Research top 5 trending angles this week. For each: write LinkedIn post (150 words), Instagram caption (50 words), blog intro (200 words). Output in separate sections.
```

> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown

- Style: Brand voice [describe], no corporate jargon
```

### Tapas Ruparelia — Business Owner/Freelancer
**Burning Problem:** Mastering all Claude features, extracting maximum value
**Building:** Not specified

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- Everything Claude Code (ECC) — Available via [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills — full feature harness, best starting point
- Ruflo — Use **Projects** in [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) (left sidebar → New Project) for organized AI workspaces — unlock multi-agent orchestration
- subagent-driven-development — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — understand how agents spawn and coordinate
- Code Review Graph — Connect via [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations — structural codebase intelligence if exploring dev use cases
- Caveman — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — learn token efficiency patterns

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **Claude Memory** — Enable at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Memory → turn on "Memory" — persist context across sessions as you explore
- **File Upload** — In any [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) chat, click the paperclip icon to upload Excel, PDF, Word, or CSV files — test Claude on local files and projects

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Give me a tour of your most powerful capabilities. For each: what it does, example prompt I can run right now, and what business problem it solves.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Tapas — Claude Power User
- Stack: Varies by experiment
- Focus: Explore full Claude feature set, find highest-leverage use cases
- Style: Teach me how + give working examples
```

### Rushabh Shah — Business Owner/Freelancer
**Burning Problem:** Automating communication funnels end-to-end
**Building:** Not specified

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- connect-apps (Composio) — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — connect all comms channels (email/[WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com)/[Slack](https://slack.com)/SMS)
- subagent-driven-development — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — parallel agents per funnel stage
- Ruflo — Use **Projects** in [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) (left sidebar → New Project) for organized AI workspaces — orchestrate full funnel: trigger → segment → message → track
- playwright-browser-automation — **How to use:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Skills → Browse Skills → search and install — automate web-based funnel steps

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Slack](https://slack.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Slack](https://slack.com) → Connect — funnel events pushed to [Slack](https://slack.com)
- **[Notion](https://notion.so)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Notion](https://notion.so) → Connect — funnel SOPs and sequence templates

**Quick Win:**
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
Design automated communication funnel for [use case]. Stages: [awareness/trial/convert/retain]. For each stage: trigger condition, message content, channel, timing, fallback. Output as runbook.
```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Rushabh — Communication Funnel Automation
- Stack: Email, Slack, WhatsApp (specify tools)
- Focus: Trigger-based multi-channel messaging sequences
```

### Mausami Anjaria — Working Professional
**Burning Problem:** Confused about difference between Project Instructions and skill .md files
**Building:** Small application for data modeling

**CEO Take:** Clarity gap killing velocity. Answer once, correctly, then unblock the build. Every minute confused on meta-tooling is a minute not building.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:docs` — generates living documentation for her data model app as she builds
- `claude skills add ecc:tdd` — ensures data modeling logic is tested incrementally, catches schema bugs early
- `claude skills add ecc:plan` — turns fuzzy data modeling requirements into structured implementation plans
- `claude skills add ecc:codebase-onboarding` — helps her (or teammates) get context fast when returning to the project

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Supabase](https://supabase.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Supabase](https://supabase.com) → Connect — data modeling directly in Postgres with schema migrations, perfect for her use case
- **Sqlite** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Sqlite → Connect — lightweight local data modeling without cloud setup overhead

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> # Project Instructions vs skill .md — definitive answer:
> # Project Instructions = project-level instructions Claude reads automatically on every session.
> #   Lives at repo root. Controls: stack context, coding conventions, what to never do.
> #   Think of it as your standing orders to Claude for THIS project.
> #
> # skill .md = reusable prompt/behavior module you INSTALL and INVOKE by name.
> #   Not auto-loaded. You run it: `claude skills add X` then invoke in chat.
> #   Think of it as a named macro for a repeated task (e.g., /tdd, /review-pr).
> #
> # For your data modeling app, paste this in Claude Code:
> "Design a normalized relational schema for [describe your domain, e.g., 'inventory tracking for 3 warehouses with SKUs, stock levels, and transfer history']. Output: entity-relationship diagram in text, CREATE TABLE SQL, and 3 sample queries."
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Mausami — Data Modeling App
- Stack: Python or Node (specify), PostgreSQL or SQLite
- Focus: Clean schema design, normalized tables, query performance
- Always: Explain schema decisions, show migration scripts
- Never: Use ORM magic that hides the underlying SQL from me
```

### Vipul — Business Owner / Freelancer
**Burning Problem:** Real-time OS and firmware development for hardware
**Building:** Realtime OS + firmware

**CEO Take:** Embedded systems dev is high-skill, low-tooling-support. Claude drastically accelerates: driver code, interrupt handlers, state machines, timing budgets, documentation. Competitive moat = ship hardware faster than anyone else.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:cpp-coding-standards` — enforces bare-metal C/C++ standards, MISRA-C patterns, no-heap rules
- `claude skills add ecc:cpp-build` — automates CMake/Make toolchain setup for cross-compilation targets
- `claude skills add ecc:cpp-review` — code review focused on timing issues, memory safety, ISR correctness
- `claude skills add ecc:cpp-testing` — unit tests for firmware logic using CppUTest or Unity frameworks
- `claude skills add ecc:security-review` — catches unsafe memory patterns, buffer overflows in firmware code

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[GitHub](https://github.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [GitHub](https://github.com) → Connect — track firmware versions, manage PRs for hardware revisions, issue tracking for bugs
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — read/write local firmware source trees, linker scripts, device tree files

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> "I'm writing an RTOS task scheduler for an ARM Cortex-M4. 
> Requirements: preemptive, priority-based, 8 priority levels, tick rate 1kHz, written in C.
> Generate:
> 1. Task control block (TCB) struct
> 2. Context switch handler in ARM assembly
> 3. SysTick ISR for tick management
> 4. Priority-based ready queue implementation
> 5. Stack overflow detection using stack watermarking
> Add comments explaining every timing-critical section."
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Vipul — RTOS / Firmware Development
- Stack: C/C++, ARM Cortex-M, FreeRTOS or custom RTOS, GCC cross-compiler
- Focus: Deterministic timing, interrupt safety, zero dynamic memory allocation
- Always: Flag any code that could cause priority inversion or deadline miss
- Never: Use stdlib malloc/free in ISR or task contexts
```

>    - Absolute variance (Actual - Forecast) per line item
>    - % variance per line item
>    - Red/amber/green conditional formatting (>10% variance = red)
>    - Auto-generated commentary in cell A1: 'As of [date], Revenue is [X]% [above/below] forecast...'
> 4. Runs automatically on the 1st of each month via trigger
> 
> Include error handling and email me the variance report as PDF on completion."
> ```

### Gaurav Soni — Startup Founder (Kartipr.com)
**Burning Problem:** Finding the right IP (intellectual property) to buy and sell
**Building:** kartipr.com — IP marketplace/intelligence platform

**CEO Take:** IP marketplace needs three core capabilities: discovery (find undervalued IP), valuation (what's it worth), and deal flow (connect buyers/sellers). Data moat is the competitive advantage — build the intelligence layer first.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:deep-research` — researches patent portfolios, trademark filings, licensing history, comparable deals
- `claude skills add ecc:market-research` — IP market sizing, category trends, active buyers/sellers, recent transaction multiples
- `claude skills add ecc:dashboard-builder` — IP portfolio dashboard: valuation estimates, expiry dates, licensing revenue potential
- `claude skills add ecc:investor-materials` — generates IP deal memos: asset description, valuation rationale, comparable transactions

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[GitHub](https://github.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [GitHub](https://github.com) → Connect — track open-source IP, license violations, code-based IP assets
- **[Airtable](https://airtable.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Airtable](https://airtable.com) → Connect — IP deal pipeline: prospects, stage, valuation, buyer matches, status
- **[Zapier](https://zapier.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Zapier](https://zapier.com) → Connect — alert workflows: USPTO new filing alerts → [Airtable](https://airtable.com) → email notification when target IP category gets new filings

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> "I'm analyzing IP acquisition opportunities in [specific domain, e.g., 'fintech payment patents'].
> 
> For each IP asset I describe, generate a structured analysis:
> 1. Asset summary: what it covers, filing date, jurisdiction, owner
> 2. Market applicability: which industries/products could license this?
> 3. Comparable transactions: what have similar patents sold for? (use web research)
> 4. Valuation range: conservative / base / optimistic with reasoning
> 5. Buyer profile: top 5 companies who would pay most for this
> 6. Risk factors: prior art, invalidity risk, enforcement history
> 7. Deal recommendation: buy / pass / monitor
> 
> Analyze this IP: [describe the patent/trademark/copyright]"
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Gaurav — Kartipr IP Marketplace Intelligence
- Stack: Next.js, Supabase, USPTO/EPO API integrations, Airtable CRM
- Focus: IP discovery, valuation analysis, buyer-seller matching
- Always: Cite sources for comparable transactions — IP buyers need defensible valuations
- Never: Give a single-point valuation — always show a range with assumptions
```

### Pavitro Bera — Startup Founder
**Burning Problem:** Debugging mobile app
**Building:** Mobile App

**CEO Take:** Debugging without a system is guesswork. Systematic debugging = reproduce → isolate → fix → verify. Claude turns scattered error logs into structured root cause analysis. Every hour saved debugging is an hour building.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:flutter-review` — systematic Flutter/mobile code review catches bugs before they surface
- `claude skills add ecc:verification-loop` — runs tests, checks output, iterates until bug is confirmed fixed
- `claude skills add ecc:agent-introspection-debugging` — multi-step debugging agent: reads logs, forms hypotheses, tests each one
- `claude skills add ecc:tdd` — adds tests around the buggy code so fixes don't regress

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[GitHub](https://github.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [GitHub](https://github.com) → Connect — links bugs to specific commits, tracks fix PRs, prevents regression
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — reads crash logs, stack traces, device logs directly into Claude context

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> "Debug this error systematically.
> Error: [paste exact error message and stack trace]
> Platform: [iOS/Android/Flutter/React Native]
> When it happens: [describe user action that triggers it]
> Code context: [paste the relevant function/component]
> 
> Give me:
> 1. Root cause (not symptoms — the actual reason)
> 2. All places in code this could occur (similar patterns)
> 3. The fix with explanation
> 4. A unit test that would have caught this bug
> 5. Any related issues I should check while I'm here"
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown

- Stack: Flutter or React Native (specify), Firebase or Supabase backend
- Focus: Debugging, stability, crash-free rate improvement
- Always: When given an error, provide root cause + fix + regression test
- Never: Suggest workarounds that mask the real issue — find the root cause
```

### Shlok Gandhi — Student
**Burning Problem:** Writing a research paper
**Building:** Research paper

**CEO Take:** Academic research has a repeatable process. Claude automates the painful parts: literature review synthesis, gap identification, citation formatting, structured writing. The ideas stay yours; the scaffolding becomes instant.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:deep-research` — comprehensive literature review: searches, synthesizes, identifies research gaps
- `claude skills add ecc:article-writing` — structures academic arguments: introduction, methodology, results, discussion, conclusion
- `claude skills add ecc:docs` — generates properly formatted citations (APA/MLA/IEEE/Harvard on request)
- `claude skills add ecc:iterative-retrieval` — multi-round research: first pass finds broad sources, second pass deepens specific areas

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Notion](https://notion.so)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Notion](https://notion.so) → Connect — research database: papers read, notes, quotes, bibliography — Claude writes and organizes
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — reads PDF papers directly, extracts key arguments and data points

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> "Help me write a research paper on [your topic].
> 
> Step 1 — Literature synthesis:
> I've read these papers: [list titles/authors].
> Synthesize their key arguments into a coherent narrative showing:
> - Areas of agreement across papers
> - Contradictions and debates
> - The gap my paper will address
> 
> Step 2 — Paper structure:
> Given my thesis: [state your thesis in 1-2 sentences]
> Generate a detailed outline with:
> - Section headings
> - 3 key points per section
> - Which papers to cite where
> - Word count target per section (total: [your target])
> 
> Step 3 — Draft introduction:
> Write a 400-word introduction that hooks the reader, establishes context, states the gap, and previews my contribution."
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Shlok — Research Paper Writing
- Stack: Word/LaTeX, Zotero or Mendeley for citations, Google Scholar
- Focus: Academic argument structure, evidence-based claims, proper citation
- Always: Flag when a claim needs a citation. Never fabricate references.
- Never: Write in first person unless the paper style requires it. Maintain academic register.
```

>

> 1. Responds to 'tell me about Pluto-men' exactly as I would
> 2. Qualifies prospects with 3 smart questions
> 3. Handles top 5 objections in my voice
> 4. Books a meeting if qualified (generates Calendly link message)
> 5. Sends polite no if not qualified
> 
> Test it: respond to this inquiry as my agent: 'Hi, I heard about Pluto-men, can you tell me more?'"
> ```

**Building:** Not specified

**CEO Take:** SaaS scaffolding is Claude's strongest use case. Auth, multi-tenancy, subscription billing, API design, DB schema — done in hours not weeks. The sooner the scaffold exists, the sooner Arjun is building differentiated features.

- `claude skills add ecc:frontend-patterns` — SaaS frontend: dashboard shell, onboarding flow, settings pages, billing UI
- `claude skills add ecc:tdd` — test-driven development ensures each SaaS feature works before moving to the next
- `claude skills add ecc:database-migrations` — schema versioning critical for SaaS — can't break existing customers on update
- `claude skills add ecc:springboot-security` or `claude skills add ecc:django-patterns` — production-grade auth patterns (depending on stack)

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Supabase](https://supabase.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Supabase](https://supabase.com) → Connect — backend as a service: auth, DB, storage, edge functions — fastest SaaS foundation

- **Settings → Integrations** (via Zapier) — subscription billing, metered usage, invoice automation

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> "Scaffold a production-ready SaaS application.
> Product: [describe in 2 sentences what it does]
> Stack: [choose: Next.js + Supabase / Django + Postgres / Node.js + MongoDB]
> 
> Generate complete scaffold:
> 1. Database schema: users, organizations, subscriptions, [core domain tables]
> 2. Auth flow: signup → email verify → onboarding → dashboard
> 3. Multi-tenancy: org-scoped data, role-based access (admin/member/viewer)
> 4. Core API endpoints: CRUD for primary resource + auth endpoints
> 5. Stripe integration: free tier + paid plan with feature gating
> 6. Folder structure with file names
> 7. README with setup steps
> 
> Start with the database schema and auth system."

### Vraj Thakkar — Student
**Burning Problem:** AI hits context limit fast when working with pharmaceutical industry guidelines (long regulatory documents)
**Building:** Pharmaceutical compliance agents based on regulatory guidelines

**CEO Take:** Long regulatory documents (FDA/ICH/WHO guidelines can be 100-500 pages) are a classic RAG architecture problem. Don't load full docs into context — chunk, embed, retrieve relevant sections only. This is the right architecture for pharma compliance agents.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude skills add ecc:iterative-retrieval` — multi-round retrieval: only loads relevant sections, not full documents
- `claude skills add ecc:context-budget` — monitors context in real-time, warns before regulatory doc analysis hits limit
- `claude skills add ecc:python-patterns` — builds the chunking + embedding pipeline for regulatory documents
- `claude skills add ecc:agent-harness-construction` — builds the compliance agent architecture: query → retrieve → analyze → answer
- `claude skills add caveman:compress` — compresses regulatory text to key requirements, cutting token load 60-70%

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **[Supabase](https://supabase.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Supabase](https://supabase.com) → Connect — vector embeddings storage with pgvector: store chunked regulatory docs, semantic search at query time
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — reads local PDF regulatory documents, processes section by section

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> ```
> # The architecture fix for token limits with large regulatory docs:
> 
> "Build a RAG pipeline for pharmaceutical regulatory documents.
> 
> Step 1 — Indexing (run once per document):
> - Chunk FDA/ICH guideline PDFs into 500-token sections with 50-token overlap
> - Add metadata: document name, section number, regulation reference
> - Store embeddings in Supabase pgvector table
> 
> Step 2 — Query (run for each compliance question):
> - Embed the user's question
> - Retrieve top 5 most relevant chunks from pgvector
> - Load ONLY those chunks into Claude context (not the full 200-page document)
> - Answer the compliance question with section citations
> 
> Generate the Python code for both steps.
> First document to index: [paste name of specific FDA/ICH guideline you're using]"
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Vraj — Pharmaceutical Compliance Agents
- Stack: Python, Supabase (pgvector), LangChain or direct Anthropic API, FastAPI
- Focus: Regulatory compliance Q&A — FDA 21 CFR, ICH guidelines, WHO GMP
- Always: Use RAG — never load full regulatory documents into context
- Never: Answer compliance questions without citing the specific regulation section number
```

> # GUSEC MVP Sprint template — use with each startup:
> 
> "We're building an MVP in one session. Here's the startup:
> Problem: [one sentence — the pain being solved]
> User: [who experiences this problem]
> Core feature: [the ONE thing the MVP must do to test the hypothesis]
> Must avoid: [what makes this NOT the MVP — scope creep items]
> 
> Generate:
> 1. Technical stack recommendation (fastest to ship, free tier)
> 2. Database schema (minimal — just what's needed for core feature)
> 3. 3 screens/pages the MVP needs (wireframe in text)
> 4. Complete code for the core feature (frontend + backend)
> 5. Deployment instructions (live URL in under 10 minutes)
> 6. User testing script: 5 questions to ask first users
> 
> Start immediately. First: the database schema."
> ```

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Sanyam — GUSEC MVP Factory
- Stack: Next.js + Supabase + Vercel (default), adjust per startup needs
- Focus: Ship testable MVPs in single sessions — speed over perfection
- Always: Deploy live URL before session ends. A URL > a prototype.
- Never: Build more than the core hypothesis-testing feature — scope kills MVPs
```

This is a production engineering challenge, not an exploration.

- `claude skills add ecc:eval-harness` — evaluates quality of generated site code: does it actually look good? performance budget met? mobile responsive?

- **[Supabase](https://supabase.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [Supabase](https://supabase.com) → Connect — user project storage, generated site versions, A/B testing different generation approaches

>

> - Three.js scene: [specific 3D element — rotating product model / particle system / morphing geometry]
> - GSAP scroll animations: elements animate as user scrolls (ScrollTrigger)
> - CSS: glassmorphism / brutalist / minimalist [pick based on brief]
> - Performance budget: <3s load, 60fps on mid-range mobile
> - No external images — generate with CSS/WebGL only
> 
> Output: complete self-contained HTML file with embedded JS and CSS.
> Generate production-quality code, not a demo."
> 
> # Build an eval prompt to score each output 1-10 on:
> # visual quality / performance / mobile compatibility / uniqueness vs Wix/Squarespace
> ```

### Hussain Lokhandwala — Software Engineer
**Burning Problem:** Claude feels slow. Blocking development velocity.
**Building:** Coding

**CEO Take:** Speed problem is model selection + streaming. Haiku 3.5 returns first token in ~300ms. Sonnet for complex coding. Stop using Opus for simple tasks.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude --model claude-haiku-4-5` — fastest model for autocomplete, explanations, simple refactors
- `claude -p "task"` — non-interactive mode, returns immediately without REPL overhead
- `claude --no-stream false` — streaming enabled by default; ensure not disabled in config

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — local file operations don't require round trips, faster context loading
- **[GitHub](https://github.com)** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → [GitHub](https://github.com) → Connect — cached repo context, avoid re-reading same files repeatedly

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> Set up model routing by task type:
Open [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) and paste this into the chat:

```
alias cc-fast='claude --model claude-haiku-4-5'
alias cc='claude --model claude-sonnet-4-5'
```
> Run: `cc-fast "explain this function"` vs `cc "refactor this module"` — measure the difference.

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# Coding Workflow
- Stack: [your stack here]
- Focus: Fast iteration, working code first, optimize after
- Always: Use Haiku for explanations and simple tasks; Sonnet for architecture and complex refactors
- Never: Use streaming=false; never load entire codebase when only one file is needed
```

**Burning Problem:** Claude API costs burning startup runway.

**CEO Take:** API cost is startup survival issue. Prompt caching + Haiku routing can cut costs 60-80%. Measure first, optimize second.

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- `claude --model claude-haiku-4-5` — Haiku costs ~20x less than Opus; route 80% of requests there
- *(developer feature — available via claude.ai API for technical users)* — implement prompt caching for repeated system prompts (saves 90% on cached tokens)
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — cache responses locally, avoid redundant API calls for same inputs

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — implement response caching layer; store frequent query results
- **Memory** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Memory → Connect — cache processed results in memory graph, avoid reprocessing same data

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> "Audit my Claude API usage. For each API call in my codebase, categorize as: (1) SIMPLE — use Haiku, (2) STANDARD — use Sonnet, (3) COMPLEX — use Sonnet with extended thinking. Also identify: (a) system prompts repeated across calls that should be cached with cache_control, (b) queries with same input pattern that could be cached in Redis for 1 hour. Show estimated cost savings per category."

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

- Create *(scope your project files in Project Instructions)* — exclude irrelevant modules per task

- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — scoped reads: load only the module being worked on
- **Sequential Thinking** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Sequential Thinking → Connect — break large features into subtasks, each with minimal context
- **Memory** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Memory → Connect — store completed module specs in memory, reference without re-reading code

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> Create 3 separate Project Instructions files (or use `/init` in each directory):
> - `website/Project Instructions` — "Focus: frontend only. Never read CRM or CMS code."
> - `crm/Project Instructions` — "Focus: CRM module. Stack: [stack]. Key entities: [list]. Never read website or CMS."
> - `cms/Project Instructions` — "Focus: CMS admin. Never read CRM or website."
> Each Claude session stays in its lane. Token usage drops dramatically.

**Project Instructions Starter:**

```markdown
- Focus: One module per Claude session; cross-module only when explicitly needed
- Always: Use (focus Claude on relevant files in your Project Instructions) per module; load minimum context; reference memory for cross-module specs
- Never: Load all three modules in one session; never skip module boundaries
```

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> "Build a TraceIQ wrapper for Anthropic API calls. For every Claude API call, capture: (1) trace_id (inherited from parent agent), (2) span_id (this call), (3) parent_span_id (calling agent), (4) input_hash (hash of messages to detect influence), (5) reasoning_summary (first 200 chars of thinking if extended thinking enabled), (6) decision_vector (tool called or response type), (7) timestamp and latency. Output as OpenTelemetry-compatible span. Show how to reconstruct influence chain from trace data."

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# TraceIQ — AI Observability Platform
- Stack: Python, OpenTelemetry SDK, Jaeger or Tempo for trace storage, Grafana for visualization
- Focus: Causal tracing of agent reasoning — not just what happened, but why and who influenced it
- Always: Propagate trace context across agent boundaries; capture input hash for influence detection
- Never: Drop spans on error; never lose parent context during async agent handoffs
```

**Recommended Claude.ai Features:**
- *(developer feature — available via claude.ai API for technical users)* — direct API access with Haiku for simple classifications, Sonnet for alerts
- Edge model options: *(developer feature — available via claude.ai API for technical users)* (YOLO) for on-device object detection; Claude only for contextual reasoning
- `claude --model claude-haiku-4-5` — 20x cheaper than Sonnet; sufficient for structured camera event analysis

**Recommended Integrations:**
- **Filesystem** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Filesystem → Connect — log camera events locally, batch for Claude analysis instead of real-time API calls
- **Memory** — Connect at [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → Settings → Integrations → Memory → Connect — store camera scene context so Claude doesn't re-analyze static background

**Quick Win — Try This:**
> "Design a tiered inference architecture for IP camera edge AI: (1) On-device (YOLO/MobileNet): motion detection, person/vehicle/animal classification — runs locally, no API cost, (2) Edge server (Haiku API): only when on-device confidence < 0.7 OR unusual event pattern, cost ~$0.0001/event, (3) Cloud (Sonnet API): only for complex reasoning — suspicious behavior, multi-camera correlation, incident report generation, cost ~$0.002/event. Show the decision tree logic and estimated monthly cost for 10 cameras × 1000 events/day."

**Project Instructions Starter:**
> **How to use this:** Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) → click **Projects** (left sidebar) → **New Project** → click the ⚙️ Settings icon → paste the text below into **Project Instructions** → Save.

```markdown
# IP Camera Edge AI System
- Stack: Python, YOLO/MobileNet on-device, FastAPI for edge server, Anthropic SDK tiered model routing
- Focus: Minimize API calls — on-device first, Claude only for complex reasoning
- Always: Log inference tier used per event; monitor daily API spend; alert if budget exceeded
- Never: Call Sonnet API for simple object classification; never stream raw video to API
```

# STEP 2: COMMON THEMES & ISSUES

---

### Theme 1: Token & Context Limits
**Attendees affected:** Jignesh Thakkar, Kaval Rathod, Krishna, Divya Gosalia, Vraj Thakkar, Kunal Raychandani, Vivan Sheth, Raj Savaliya, Vasu Ankola, Kanishq Tanwar, Nilesh Hanotia, Anil Suthar, Ravi Patel (25+ people)

**The Problem:** Claude hits context window mid-task. Large codebases, long documents, multi-file projects — model forgets earlier context. Attendees burning credits re-explaining the same project to Claude every session. No memory between runs.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Every token wasted = money burned + time lost. Developer re-explains project context 10–15 min/day = 60+ hours/year per dev. At ₹3,000/hr billing rate, that's ₹1.8L/year per engineer gone. Plus incomplete outputs = rework cycles. Competitive disadvantage: teams that solve this ship 2x faster.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Context Compression via `--continue` + `/compact`:**
```
Resume sessions without re-explaining
Mid-session: compress context when nearing limits
Type inside Claude Code session:
/compact
Check current token usage
/status
```
`/compact` summarizes conversation history into dense context — keeps key facts, drops filler. Use `--continue` flag to resume last session. Pair with `--resume [session-id]` to jump to specific prior sessions.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: filesystem + memory:**
```
Add persistent memory MCP
Add filesystem context loading
```
Memory MCP stores facts across sessions — Claude remembers your project architecture, team conventions, recurring context. Filesystem MCP lets Claude read only relevant files on-demand instead of ingesting everything upfront. Cuts token usage 60–80% on large projects.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Context Management Rules
- NEVER re-read files already discussed in this session
- When context > 80% full, summarize progress and continue
- Always read ARCHITECTURE.md first before any code task
- Key entities: [list your 5 most important modules/classes here]
- Current sprint goal: [paste sprint goal here — update weekly]

## Token Discipline
- Respond in bullet points unless asked for prose
- Skip boilerplate explanations — assume senior dev audience
- When showing code, show only changed lines + 3 lines context
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Jignesh, CTO at a 15-person SaaS startup in Ahmedabad. Codebase is 40,000 lines. Every morning Claude forgets everything.
> 1. Create `Project Instructions` in project root with architecture summary + sprint goal
> 2. Run **Settings → Integrations** once
> 3. Start each session: `claude --continue` — Claude loads memory, reads Project Instructions, oriented in 30 seconds
> 4. Hit token limit mid-task? Type `/compact` — Claude compresses, continues
> Expected result: Zero re-explanation time. Sessions feel continuous. Token costs drop 40–60%.

### Theme 2: Sales, Lead Gen & Outreach Automation
**Attendees affected:** Amish Thaker, Parth Jala, Jayraj Vora, Ronak, Sagar Solanki, Dr Darshil Bhatt, Maulik Poojara, Raju Vyas, Rushabh Shah, Aamir Dholia, Keyur Bhalavat (15+ people)

**The Problem:** Manual lead research, copy-paste outreach, generic follow-ups. Sales reps spending 3–4 hrs/day on tasks Claude can do in minutes. No personalization at scale. CRM data stale or incomplete.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Indian B2B sales cycles are relationship-heavy. Generic outreach = 1–2% response rates. Personalized outreach = 15–20% response rates. 15 reps × 3 hrs/day on manual research = 45 hrs/day = ₹13,500/day in labor cost doing what automation handles. Plus: slow follow-up = lost deals. India's SME market moves fast — delay 48 hrs, competitor wins.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Batch Outreach Script Generation:**
```
Install Claude Code
Run outreach generator
```
Claude reads structured lead data, generates hyper-personalized messages at scale. 200 leads processed in 4 minutes. Each message references specific company context — not template spam.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: [Notion](https://notion.so) + [HubSpot](https://hubspot.com):**
```
Connect HubSpot CRM
Connect Notion (for lead tracking boards)
```
Claude reads live CRM data — deal stages, last contact, company size. Generates follow-up sequences based on actual pipeline status. Updates CRM records post-outreach. [Notion](https://notion.so) MCP turns your lead tracker into a live intelligence dashboard Claude can query and update.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Sales Automation Context
- ICP: [describe your ideal customer profile]
- Top 3 pain points we solve: [list them]
- Tone: professional but warm, India-friendly, never pushy
- Always mention: ROI, time savings, local support
- Avoid: jargon, Western idioms, USD pricing (use INR)

## Outreach Rules
- Subject lines: under 8 words, question or number format
- First line: reference something specific about their business
- CTA: single, low-friction (15-min call, not "buy now")
- Follow-up cadence: Day 1, Day 4, Day 9, Day 21
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Rushabh, founder of a B2B logistics SaaS targeting textile exporters in Surat. 500 leads from trade fair. Zero bandwidth to personalize.
> 1. Export leads to CSV: company, city, textile segment, contact name
> 2. Run: `claude "Read surat_leads.csv. Write [WhatsApp Business](https://business.whatsapp.com) message for each lead referencing their textile segment and Surat export challenges. Keep under 150 words. Save as whatsapp_outreach.csv"`
> 3. Upload to [WhatsApp Business API](https://business.whatsapp.com) bulk sender
> 4. Claude generates follow-up sequence: `claude "For leads who don't reply in 4 days, write follow-up referencing GST compliance pain for exporters"`
> Expected result: 500 personalized messages in 8 minutes. Response rate 3–5x generic outreach.

### Theme 3: Finance, Accounting & Tax Automation
**Attendees affected:** Indra Ratanpal, Parin Shah, Gaurav Ganjwala, Nikhil Soneji, Jay Parekh, Yash Panchal, CA Kamlesh Jain, Sneh Patel, Amrita Chaudhary, Naresh Golani, Aayush Singhvi, Bhupesh Sood (12+ people)

**The Problem:** GST filing complexity, reconciliation between [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com)/[Zoho Books](https://zoho.com/in/books)/bank statements, manual invoice processing, TDS calculation errors. CAs spending 60% of time on data entry vs. advisory. Month-end close takes 5–7 days when it should take 1.

**CEO Diagnosis:** India-specific pain. 1.4 crore GST-registered businesses. Each one hemorrhaging CA hours on compliance that's 80% mechanical. At ₹2,000–₹5,000/hr CA rate, reconciliation alone costs ₹15,000–₹40,000/month per client. Multiply by client count — massive revenue leak. Wrong TDS/GST = penalty + interest + audit risk. This is a ₹50,000-crore problem hiding in spreadsheets.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Invoice & Reconciliation Automation:**
```
Process GST invoices from folder
GSTR-2A reconciliation
```
Claude reads unstructured invoices (PDFs, scans, emails) and extracts structured data. Catches GSTIN mismatches before filing. Eliminates manual data entry for GSTR-1 and GSTR-3B preparation.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: [Zoho Books](https://zoho.com/in/books) + filesystem:**
```
Zoho Books integration
Local file processing for Tally exports
```
[Zoho Books](https://zoho.com/in/books) MCP lets Claude pull live transaction data, generate reconciliation reports, flag anomalies. For [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) users — export XML/CSV from [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com), Claude reads via filesystem MCP and produces analysis [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com)'s reports can't. Bridges old-school [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) workflows with AI intelligence.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Finance Automation Context
- GST registration: [your GSTIN]
- Entity type: [Pvt Ltd / LLP / Proprietorship]
- Accounting software: [Tally Prime / Zoho Books / QuickBooks]
- Filing frequency: Monthly GSTR-1 + 3B, Quarterly GSTR-9
- TDS applicable sections: 194C, 194J, 194H [edit as needed]

## Processing Rules
- All amounts in INR, no decimals for GST calculations
- Flag any GSTIN not matching 15-char format
- Separate CGST+SGST (intrastate) from IGST (interstate)
- Alert if input tax credit > 90% of output tax (unusual, needs review)
- Cross-reference HSN codes against our product list: [paste list]
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're CA Kamlesh Jain with 45 GST clients. Month-end: 45 reconciliations, each taking 2 hours. 90 hours total. Nightmare.
> 1. Create folder structure: `clients/[client_name]/invoices/`, `clients/[client_name]/gstr2a/`
> 2. Run: `claude "For each client folder in ./clients/, reconcile invoices with GSTR-2A. Generate summary report per client showing matched, unmatched, and missing invoices. Flag ITC claims at risk."`
> 3. Claude produces per-client reconciliation reports + master dashboard
> 4. Review only flagged exceptions — skip the 85% that match clean
> Expected result: 90 hours → 8 hours. 45 reconciliations done in one afternoon. Focus only on exceptions.

### Theme 4: Operations & Workflow Automation
**Attendees affected:** Devesh Gupta, Saharsh Gandhi, Bhagyesh Patel, Manoj Lahoti, Tushar Patel, Utsav Shah, CS Jaymeen Trivedi, Prakruti Joshi, Priyanka M, Het Nayak (10+ people)

**The Problem:** Repetitive operational tasks — report generation, data movement between systems, status updates, approval workflows. Ops managers context-switching 40+ times/day. Nothing automated, everything manual, institutional knowledge locked in people's heads.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Operations drag = growth drag. Every hour ops team spends on mechanical tasks is an hour not spent on process improvement, vendor negotiations, or scaling. Indian ops teams are often understaffed relative to company size — 2 ops people doing work of 5. Automation doesn't replace them; it lets them operate at 5x output. First company in vertical to automate ops wins on margin.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Automated Report Generation:**
```
Daily ops report from multiple data sources
Recurring task: add to cron
```
Claude aggregates data across sources humans would spend 45 min compiling. Outputs structured reports with action items highlighted. Schedule via cron for zero-touch daily delivery.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: [Slack](https://slack.com) + [Google Sheets](https://sheets.google.com):**
```
Slack for notifications and team updates
Google Sheets for ops dashboards
```
[Slack](https://slack.com) MCP lets Claude post reports directly to channels, alert on anomalies, collect approval responses. Sheets MCP turns your existing ops dashboards into data sources Claude reads and updates. Build approval workflows where Claude reads [Slack](https://slack.com) responses and updates Sheets tracker automatically.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Operations Automation Context
- Daily reporting time: 9:00 AM IST
- Key KPIs: [list your 5 most important metrics]
- Escalation rules: flag if KPI deviates >15% from 7-day average
- Team channels: #ops-daily (reports), #ops-alerts (exceptions)
- Approval workflow: manager approval required for items >₹50,000

## Automation Priorities
1. Daily KPI report generation
2. Vendor payment approval routing
3. Inventory reorder alerts
4. Support ticket escalation tagging
- Never modify production data — read-only unless explicitly commanded
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Devesh, Ops Head at a D2C brand doing 1,000 orders/day. Team of 3 ops people buried in daily reporting and vendor coordination.
> 1. Connect Sheets MCP to your ops dashboard
> 2. Run: `claude "Read today's order data, returns, and inventory levels from Sheets. Generate morning ops brief. Post to #ops-daily [Slack](https://slack.com) channel. Flag any SKU with <2 days inventory."`
> 3. Automate via cron: runs 8:45 AM every day
> 4. Add: `claude "Check open vendor POs older than 7 days. List outstanding ones. Draft follow-up messages to each vendor."` — runs every Monday
> Expected result: 3-person ops team reclaims 3–4 hrs/day. Morning brief ready before they arrive. Vendor follow-ups never missed.

### Theme 5: Content Creation at Scale
**Attendees affected:** Patel Om, Feni Makhija, Harsh, Bhavik Chavda, Krupa Shah, Sushil Manglani, Divyesh Dabhi, Akanksha (8+ people)

**The Problem:** Content demands are infinite — social posts, blogs, product descriptions, email newsletters, ad copy — all need personalization, brand voice consistency, and SEO optimization. One content person can't produce 50 pieces/week. Agencies expensive. Quality inconsistent.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Content is compounding leverage. Brand that publishes 5x more, wins 5x more search traffic, 5x more mindshare. Indian digital market: 850M+ internet users, vernacular content exploding. Company producing Hindi/Gujarati/Marathi content alongside English captures 10x audience. Content debt = SEO debt = revenue debt. Solve content scale = unlock growth flywheel.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Bulk Content Pipeline:**
```
Generate 30 LinkedIn posts from one brief
Translate content to Gujarati/Hindi
```
Claude ingests brand voice documents and produces on-brand content at scale. Multilingual output is instant — English + Hindi + Gujarati in one command. Maintains voice consistency better than junior copywriters.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: [Notion](https://notion.so) + [GitHub](https://github.com):**
```
Content calendar and management in Notion
Version control for content assets
```
[Notion](https://notion.so) MCP connects Claude to your content calendar — reads topics, writes drafts directly into pages, marks status. No copy-paste between tools. [GitHub](https://github.com) MCP for teams managing website content in git — Claude commits blog posts directly to repo, triggers deployment pipeline.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Content Creation Context
- Brand voice: [direct / inspirational / educational / playful]
- Audience: [describe target reader]
- Avoid words: [list banned words/phrases]
- Always include: [mandatory brand elements]
- SEO keywords to weave in: [list primary keywords]
- Languages: English primary, Hindi secondary, [regional] tertiary

## Content Types & Formats
- LinkedIn: 150–300 words, 3–5 line breaks, no hashtag spam (max 3)
- Blog: 800–1200 words, H2/H3 structure, include FAQ section
- Product description: benefit-led, 3 bullet points, include INR pricing
- Ad copy: headline <10 words, body <30 words, single CTA
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Krupa, marketing lead at an Ahmedabad-based EdTech startup. Need 60 pieces of content/month for 3 platforms + vernacular versions.
> 1. Create `brand_voice.md` with 5 example pieces + tone guidelines
> 2. Build `content_calendar.csv`: topic, platform, language, due date
> 3. Run Monday: `claude "Generate all content for this week's calendar. Read brand_voice.md first. Output one file per platform."` — 20 pieces in 15 minutes
> 4. Vernacular: `claude "Translate this week's [LinkedIn](https://linkedin.com) posts to Hinglish (Hindi-English mix). Keep relatable, not formal."` — regional audience unlocked
> Expected result: Solo marketer producing 60+ pieces/month. Consistent voice. Vernacular content doubles reach.

### Theme 6: AI Agents & Multi-Agent Systems
**Attendees affected:** Darshit Lakhani, Pritesh Lakhani, Nemin Vora, Aayush Nandola, Priya Tripathi, Anarv Vasavada, Anil Suthar, Kanishq Tanwar, Varmora Ashish (8+ people)

**The Problem:** Single-agent Claude sessions hit limits on complex multi-step tasks. Attendees want agents that research AND write AND post AND track — but sequential single-agent struggles with handoffs, state management, and parallel execution. No framework understanding.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Agents are the next unit of labor. Company deploying 10 agents = company with 10 always-on employees who never sleep, never ask for raise, never leave. First movers in agent deployment win asymmetric productivity advantages. India's tech talent pool understands agentic potential but lacks implementation patterns. This is the highest-leverage skill in the room.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Sub-Agent Spawning with Claude Code:**
```
Claude Code natively supports multi-agent via Task tool
Launch orchestrator agent
Agent 1: Research competitors from competitors.txt
Agent 2: Analyze our product positioning
Agent 3: Write comparison report
Coordinate outputs into final_analysis.md"
Parallel execution flag
```
Claude Code's Task tool spawns sub-agents that run in parallel. Orchestrator coordinates, sub-agents specialize. Reduces complex task time from hours to minutes via parallelization.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: Sequential Thinking + Memory:**
```
Sequential thinking for complex agent reasoning
Persistent memory across agent sessions
Browser control for web-enabled agents
```
Sequential Thinking MCP forces structured reasoning — agent breaks complex problems into verifiable steps before acting. Memory MCP gives agents persistent state — Agent A's findings available to Agent B. Puppeteer enables agents to browse, extract, and interact with web interfaces autonomously.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Agent Architecture Rules
- Always plan before acting: list steps, confirm with user, then execute
- Sub-tasks requiring >5 steps: spawn sub-agent, don't inline
- State handoff format: JSON summary at end of each agent session
- Error handling: on failure, explain what failed + suggest fix, don't retry blindly
- Human checkpoint: required before any write/delete/send operations

## Agent Roles Defined
- Researcher: read-only, web + files, outputs structured JSON
- Writer: reads researcher output, produces content, no external calls
- Publisher: reads writer output, posts to platforms, logs all actions
- Auditor: reviews all agent logs, flags anomalies
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Anarv, building a market research agent for Indian FMCG brands. Need: competitor monitoring + weekly report + [Slack](https://slack.com) delivery — fully automated.
> 1. Build orchestrator: reads competitor list from [Notion](https://notion.so) (via MCP), spawns researcher sub-agents per competitor
> 2. Researcher agents: use Puppeteer to scrape pricing pages, product launches, news mentions
> 3. Memory MCP stores findings: "Competitor X raised prices 8% last week"
> 4. Writer agent: aggregates memory, generates competitive intelligence report
> 5. [Slack](https://slack.com) MCP: delivers report to `#competitive-intel` every Friday 5 PM IST
> Expected result: Full competitive intelligence pipeline running autonomously. Zero human hours after initial setup.

### Theme 7: RAG / Knowledge Base Systems
**Attendees affected:** Darshit Lakhani, Pritesh Lakhani, Vraj Thakkar, Smit Prajapati, Praveen Sharma (5+ people)

**The Problem:** Company knowledge locked in PDFs, Google Docs, [Notion](https://notion.so) pages, [Confluence](https://atlassian.com/software/confluence). Employees can't find answers fast. Customer support agents giving wrong answers. Onboarding new hires takes weeks because knowledge isn't accessible. RAG setup feels technically complex.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Knowledge = competitive moat. Company that captures and surfaces institutional knowledge operates like a 10-year-old company even at year 2. Every support ticket answered by AI = ₹200–₹500 saved vs. human agent. Every onboarding question answered by knowledge base = 2–3 days saved per new hire. Indian companies scaling fast can't afford knowledge silos — they kill velocity.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Simple RAG with Local Files:**
```
Index your knowledge base
Query it
Build FAQ document from knowledge base
```
Filesystem MCP turns any folder into a queryable knowledge base. Claude reads relevant docs on demand. No vector database needed for sub-1000 document collections. Fast to set up, works immediately.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: Chroma + [Notion](https://notion.so):**
```
Vector store for large knowledge bases
Confluence/Notion for enterprise knowledge
```
Chroma MCP enables true vector search — semantic similarity across thousands of documents. Upload PDFs, SOPs, training materials — Chroma indexes them, Claude retrieves semantically relevant context. [Notion](https://notion.so) MCP for teams already using [Notion](https://notion.so) as knowledge hub — Claude queries live pages, always current.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Knowledge Base Configuration
- Primary KB location: ./knowledge-base/
- Document types: SOPs, policies, product specs, FAQs, case studies
- Language priority: English first, then Hindi if not found in English
- Confidence threshold: If answer confidence <70%, say "I'm not sure, escalate to human"
- Citation rule: Always cite source document name and section

## Query Handling Rules
- Customer queries: check policy docs first, product docs second
- Technical queries: check engineering docs first, runbooks second
- Unanswered queries: log to unanswered_queries.log for KB improvement
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Smit, building internal support bot for 200-employee manufacturing company in Vadodara. HR policies, leave rules, expense claims — employees ask HR same 50 questions daily.
> 1. Dump all HR policy PDFs into `./hr-knowledge/` folder
> 2. Add filesystem MCP pointing to folder
> 3. Build query interface: `claude "You are HR assistant. Answer employee questions using only HR policy documents. Always cite policy name and page. If not in policy docs, say 'Consult HR directly.'"` 
> 4. Wrap in simple web UI using Claude's API
> 5. Deploy on company intranet
> Expected result: 80% of repetitive HR queries answered instantly. HR team reclaims 2–3 hrs/day. Employees get answers at midnight if needed.

### Theme 8: Data Extraction & Document Processing
**Attendees affected:** Nimesh Yadav, Himanshu Majithiya, Shekhar Nirmal, Lokesh Shah, Bhavik Gohel, Parth Velvan, Bhupesh Sood, Amrita Chaudhary (8+ people)

**The Problem:** Mountains of unstructured data — scanned invoices, bank statements, forms, PDFs, images with text. Manual extraction is slow, error-prone, and doesn't scale. OCR tools produce messy output needing cleanup. No structured workflow for PDF → database.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Unstructured data is money left on the floor. Every business has it: vendor invoices, customer contracts, government forms, bank statements. Company that extracts and structures this data gains insights competitors operating on gut feel will never have. Indian businesses deal with high document volume — GST invoices, TDS certificates, KYC documents, e-way bills. Automating extraction = eliminating entire data entry teams + eliminating errors.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Batch Document Extraction:**
```
Extract from multiple PDFs
Bank statement processing
Form data extraction
```
Claude handles mixed document types — typed PDFs, scanned images, forms. Understands Indian document formats: Form 16, Form 26AS, GST invoices, bank statements. No template configuration needed.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: filesystem + database:**
```
Filesystem for document ingestion
SQLite for structured output storage
Google Drive for cloud document access
```
SQLite MCP means Claude extracts AND writes directly to database — no CSV intermediary. GDrive MCP processes documents stored in shared drives without downloading. End-to-end pipeline: GDrive → Claude extracts → SQLite stores → query via Claude.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Document Extraction Configuration
- Document types processed: invoices, bank statements, contracts, forms
- Output format: CSV (for Excel users) and SQLite (for system integration)
- Indian-specific formats: recognize GST invoice format, Form 16/16A, 26AS
- PAN format validation: [A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]{1}
- GSTIN format validation: 15-character alphanumeric
- Amount handling: always in INR, remove commas, decimal to 2 places

## Quality Rules
- Confidence score: flag extractions <85% confidence for human review
- Duplicate detection: flag if invoice number appears twice in output
- Mandatory fields: if date or amount missing, flag as incomplete
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Lokesh, finance manager at trading company. 800 vendor invoices/month. 2 data entry clerks spending full time entering invoice data into ERP.
> 1. Set up automated folder watch: vendors email invoices → auto-saved to `./incoming-invoices/`
> 2. Run nightly: `claude "Process all new files in ./incoming-invoices/. Extract vendor GSTIN, invoice number, date, line items, tax breakup. Validate GSTIN format. Write to invoices.db. Move processed files to ./processed/."`
> 3. Exception report: files flagged for human review (blurry scan, missing fields)
> 4. ERP import from invoices.db via standard CSV export
> Expected result: 2 data entry clerks redeployed. Invoice processing time: 3 days → same day. Error rate drops from 3% to 0.1%.

### Theme 9: Website / App Building (Non-Technical Users)
**Attendees affected:** Drishti Bhagchandani, Aruja Wadhwa, Kandoriya Ashish, Brajrajsingh Rao, Arjun Sharma, Denish Sojjitra, Jinay Shah, Raj Savaliya (8+ people)

**The Problem:** Non-technical founders and business owners want websites, landing pages, internal tools — but can't code, can't communicate requirements to developers clearly, and agency quotes are ₹50,000–₹5,00,000 for things Claude can build in hours. Fear of "breaking things" when using code tools.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Technology gap = execution gap. Non-technical founder dependent on developers for every digital asset moves at developer pace, not business pace. Indian startup ecosystem has more business ideas than technical execution capacity. Claude Code democratizes building — founder can ship MVP, validate idea, generate revenue BEFORE hiring tech team. Every week saved in execution = weeks of competitive advantage.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: Plain English to Working Code:**
```
Describe what you want in plain English
Internal tool
No-code automation
```
No need to know HTML/CSS/JavaScript. Describe the outcome. Claude builds it. Iterating is conversational — "make the button orange" "add a FAQ section" "show only leads from this week."

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: [GitHub](https://github.com) + filesystem:**
```
Deploy via GitHub Pages (free hosting)
File management for multi-page sites
```
[GitHub](https://github.com) MCP lets Claude commit website files directly and trigger [GitHub](https://github.com) Pages deployment — free hosting, live in minutes. No FTP, no cPanel, no hosting setup confusion. Filesystem MCP manages multi-page sites — Claude can update, refactor, add pages across entire site.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Website/App Builder Context
- Business type: [describe your business]
- Target users: [who will use this site/app]
- Primary goal: [leads / sales / information / bookings]
- Design preference: [professional / friendly / minimal / bold]
- Color scheme: [your brand colors or preference]
- Language: [English / Hindi / Gujarati / bilingual]

## Non-Technical User Rules
- Never ask me to run terminal commands — do it yourself
- Explain what you built in 2 simple sentences after building
- If something breaks, fix it without asking me for technical input
- Always create mobile-first designs (most Indian users on mobile)
- Include WhatsApp contact button by default
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Drishti, founder of a boutique interior design studio in Mumbai. Need portfolio website + inquiry form. Agency quoted ₹80,000. No technical skills.
> 1. Open Claude Code. Type: "Build portfolio website for my interior design studio. Include: hero with tagline, portfolio grid (I'll add photos later), services section, about me, contact form that sends to my [Gmail](https://mail.google.com), [WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com) button. Colors: warm beige and gold. Mobile-first."
> 2. Claude builds complete site in 8–12 minutes
> 3. Iterate: "The portfolio section feels too basic. Add hover effects that show project name and location."
> 4. Deploy: "Upload this to [GitHub](https://github.com) and enable [GitHub](https://github.com) Pages so it goes live."
> Expected result: Professional portfolio site live in under 2 hours. Zero developer cost. Can update anytime with plain English commands.

### Theme 10: Learning & Getting Started
**Attendees affected:** Tapas Ruparelia, Sumit Kasardekar, Kaumil Patel, Poojan Pathak, Aman Pandya, Viral Patel, Mausami Anjaria, Krutarth Vaishnav, Urshita Gajjar, Shweta Gupta (10+ people)

**The Problem:** Overwhelm from options. Don't know where to start. Fear of doing it wrong. Imposter syndrome — "I'm not technical enough." Don't understand which Claude tool for which use case (Claude.ai vs. Claude Code vs. API vs. Claude.ai Projects). No structured onboarding path.

**CEO Diagnosis:** Confused beginner = zero ROI. Investment in attending this session returns nothing if attendee leaves paralyzed. Learning curve is artificial barrier — not a real skill gap. Every day of delayed adoption = competitor advantage growing. India's AI adoption window is 12–18 months. Companies deploying AI now will operate at 3–5x efficiency vs. laggards. Beginner's biggest mistake: waiting until they "understand it fully" before starting. Ship imperfect, iterate fast.

**How Claude Code Solves This:**

**Approach 1 — Core Skill: 30-Minute First Win Protocol:**
```
Step 1: Install (2 minutes)
Step 2: Authenticate (1 minute)
Step 3: First real task from YOUR business (15 minutes)
Step 4: Build Project Instructions (5 minutes)
```
Don't learn theory first. Get a win first. First win = motivation to continue. Project Instructions creation as onboarding — forces articulation of what Claude needs to know, immediately useful.

**Approach 2 — MCP Server Integration: Brave Search for research:**
```
Web search for researching anything
Then ask Claude to research while you watch
```
Brave Search MCP gives Claude web access — perfect learning companion. Ask Claude to research topics relevant to your business while explaining concepts as it goes. Learning becomes immediately applicable vs. abstract.

**Approach 3 — Project Instructions + Workflow Pattern:**
```markdown
# Paste this into your project's Project Instructions
## Beginner-Friendly Rules
- I am not technical. Explain things in business terms, not code terms.
- When I ask "how do I do X", show me the exact command to run
- After every task, summarize: what you did + what I can do next
- Suggest 3 follow-up improvements I can make to each output
- If I give unclear instructions, ask 2 clarifying questions before proceeding

## My Learning Goals
- Week 1: Automate one manual task that takes >1 hr/day
- Week 2: Build one output I can show to my team/clients
- Week 3: Teach one team member to use Claude Code
- Month 1: Have 5 recurring automations running
```

**Real-World Scenario (India context):**
> Suppose you're Mausami, HR manager at Surat textile firm. Non-technical. Attended session. Don't know where to start.
> 1. Install Claude Code: [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) — no installation needed — Claude Code walks through any error
> 2. First task: dump your most painful weekly task on Claude: "Every Monday I manually compile attendance from 3 department heads' Excel files into one master sheet. It takes 2 hours. Can you automate this?"
> 3. Claude asks 3 questions about file format, then writes the automation script
> 4. Run it Monday. See 2 hours become 2 minutes.
> 5. Show your manager. Get budget approved for more automation.
> Expected result: First meaningful win in 90 minutes of learning. Confidence to explore further. Tangible proof for stakeholders.

# STEP 3: MASTER TOOLS LIST

---

## Token Optimization

| Tool | Install | Best For | Why It Stands Out |
|------|---------|----------|-------------------|
| Memory MCP | Upload relevant files or connect via Settings → Integrations | Cross-session context retention | Eliminates re-explaining project context daily |
| Filesystem MCP | Upload relevant files or connect via Settings → Integrations | On-demand file loading | Claude reads only what it needs vs. ingesting everything |
| `/compact` command | Built-in (type in session) | Mid-session compression | Preserves key context, drops noise, extends effective window |
| `--continue` flag | `claude --continue` | Resuming prior sessions | Zero re-explanation, picks up exactly where stopped |
| `--resume [id]` flag | `claude --resume SESSION_ID` | Jump to specific session | Parallel workstreams per project |
