# STEP 4: GETTING STARTED WITH CLAUDE.AI — NO TERMINAL NEEDED

---

## Step 1: Open Claude.ai

Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) in your browser. Sign up free or log in. No installation required.

---

## Step 2: Start a Conversation

Click **"New chat"** and just type what you need. Examples:
- "Help me write a sales email for [my product]"
- "Analyse this spreadsheet and tell me which products are most profitable" (then upload the file)
- "Write 10 [Instagram](https://instagram.com) captions for my [business type]"
- "Summarise this PDF and pull out the key action items" (then upload the file)

---

## Step 3: Create a Project (Your AI Workspace)

1. Click **Projects** in the left sidebar
2. Click **New Project** and give it a name (e.g. "Sales Automation" or "Content Creation")
3. Click the ⚙️ Settings icon → add instructions about your business in **Project Instructions**
4. Now every chat in this Project remembers your context — no re-explaining every time

**Example Project Instructions to paste:**
```
I run a [type of business] in [city].
My customers are [describe your customers].
Always write in a [professional/friendly/casual] tone.
Use INR for all prices.
Keep outputs concise and actionable.
```

---

## Step 4: Connect Your Tools

Go to **Settings → Integrations** and connect:
- **[Google Drive](https://drive.google.com)** — Claude can read your files and docs
- **[Gmail](https://mail.google.com)** — Claude can draft emails and summarise threads
- **[Google Calendar](https://calendar.google.com)** — Claude can check your schedule and draft invites
- **[GitHub](https://github.com)** — Claude can review code and manage repositories
- **[Notion](https://notion.so)** — Claude can read and write your workspace docs

---

## Step 5: Upload Files for Analysis

In any chat, click the **paperclip icon** (📎):
- Upload Excel files → ask Claude to analyse and find insights
- Upload PDFs → ask Claude to summarise or extract data
- Upload Word docs → ask Claude to edit, rewrite, or restructure
- Upload images → ask Claude to describe or analyse them

---

## Power Phrases That Work

```
HOW TO GET BETTER RESULTS FROM CLAUDE:

Be specific about:
- WHAT you want: "Build a landing page" not "help me with website"
- WHO it's for: "My customers are small shop owners in Ahmedabad"
- WHAT FORMAT: "Output as a table" / "Write as bullet points" / "Give me a draft email"
- WHAT TO AVOID: "Don't use technical language" / "Keep prices in INR"

POWER PHRASES TO USE:
- "I'm not technical. Explain in simple terms."
- "Give me a step-by-step plan."
- "After this, tell me what you created in 2 sentences."
- "What are 3 ways I can improve this next?"
- "Something isn't right. Here's the issue: [describe]. Please fix it."

EXAMPLE PROMPTS THAT WORK (paste directly into claude.ai):
- "I run a travel agency. Create a customer welcome email that I can send to new clients. Professional but warm tone."
- "I've uploaded my sales data. Tell me which product sold best last month and explain why in simple terms."
- "Write 10 LinkedIn posts for my accounting firm targeting small business owners in Gujarat. Professional tone, mention GST expertise."
- "My team spends an hour every Monday compiling a report. I'll paste the data here — create a clear summary report for my manager."
```

---

## India-Specific Quick Wins

Paste these directly into [claude.ai](https://claude.ai) chat:

**GST & Finance:**
- "I'll paste my invoice data below. Extract: GSTIN, invoice number, taxable value, CGST, SGST, IGST. Flag any issues."
- "Here's my P&L for FY2024 [paste or upload]. Generate a management summary letter in professional format."
- "Generate a GST compliance calendar for FY2025 with all key filing due dates."

**Sales & Outreach:**
- "I have a sales call with [company] tomorrow. Research them and give me: 5-bullet brief, 3 discovery questions, and 2 likely objection responses."
- "Write a 5-touch email nurture sequence for [my target customer]. Each email: subject line + 100-word body."

**Content:**
- "Write this product description in both English and Gujarati. Keep the same meaning, adjust idioms for local context."
- "Generate 30 days of [WhatsApp Business](https://business.whatsapp.com) broadcast content for my retail store — mix of offers, tips, and engagement posts."

**Operations:**
- "Here are my team's task updates [paste]. Create a clear status report for my weekly review meeting."
- "Draft a standard freelancer contract for India. Include: payment terms, IP ownership, confidentiality, jurisdiction [city]. Plain language."

---

## Using Deep Research

For in-depth research, click **"Deep Research"** in the claude.ai chat:
- "Research the top 5 competitors in [your industry] in India. Compare their pricing, features, and target market."
- "Find the latest GST filing requirements for e-commerce companies in India."
- "Research market size for [your product category] in India with data sources."


---

# STEP 5: TROUBLESHOOTING — CLAUDE.AI BROWSER VERSION

---

## Common Problems & Fixes

| Problem | Solution |
|---------|----------|
| Claude gives generic, unhelpful answers | Be more specific. Add context: "I run a [type] business in [city]. My customers are [describe]." Use a Project with saved Project Instructions. |
| Response feels incomplete or cut off | Type: "Please continue from where you left off." Or: "Output this in sections — pause and ask me to confirm before continuing." |
| Conversation getting too long or confusing | Start a new chat inside your Project — Project Instructions are automatically remembered. Or type: "Let's start fresh. My context is: [brief summary]." |
| Claude seems to forget what I told it | Use **Projects** (left sidebar in claude.ai) to save your business context permanently. Or turn on **Memory** in Settings → Memory. |
| I accidentally closed my chat | Your conversations are saved automatically. Click the chat history icon in the left sidebar to find your previous chats. |
| Uploaded file is not being analysed properly | Make sure the file is a supported format (PDF, Excel .xlsx, Word .docx, CSV, images). For scanned PDFs, copy the text manually or use a phone scanner app for a clearer scan. |
| India bank statement PDF not working well | Export as CSV from your net banking portal instead of PDF — Claude handles CSV much better. Upload the CSV file using the paperclip icon. |
| GST portal data not being read correctly | Copy and paste the data directly into the chat, and add: "This is GSTR-2A data from the GST portal. Date format is DD/MM/YYYY." |
| Output not matching my business tone | Create a Project and add your brand voice in Project Instructions: "Always write in a [tone] style. My brand values are [values]." |
| Not sure if Claude output is accurate | Always have a qualified professional (CA, lawyer, doctor) review financial, legal, or medical outputs. Claude is a first-draft tool, not a final authority. |
| Claude writes in English but I need Gujarati or Hindi | Add to your prompt: "Translate this output to [Gujarati/Hindi]. Keep brand names and product names in English." |
| Cannot pay Anthropic with Indian card | Anthropic accepts international Visa/Mastercard/Amex. Best options: Niyo Global card, Scapia card, HDFC Regalia — all support international transactions with low forex markup. RuPay often does not work. |
| Integration not connecting (Google, [Slack](https://slack.com), Notion) | Go to Settings → Integrations → find the service → click Disconnect then Connect again. Make sure you are logged into that service in your browser first. |
| Cannot find the Projects feature | Projects is in the left sidebar of claude.ai (desktop view). Log in at claude.ai and look for "Projects" in the left panel. |
| Deep Research not appearing | Deep Research is available on Claude Pro plan. Upgrade at claude.ai → Settings → Plan. |
| Claude gives a wrong answer about my specific business | Claude does not know your business by default. Add your business details to your Project Instructions — then every chat in that Project has your context. |
| I do not know how to start | Go to [claude.ai](https://claude.ai), sign up free, and type exactly what you need help with. Start simple: "Help me write an email to a new client introducing my business." |


---

## Session Day Facilitator Notes

### Pre-Session Checklist
- Test the projector and make sure claude.ai loads properly in the browser
- Have QR code or short link to claude.ai ready to share with attendees
- Share link to claude.ai — attendees can sign up free right away
- Have a Claude Pro account logged in for live demos
- Have Project Instructions template printed / shareable via [WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com) group

### Top 10 Questions From This Audience — Answers Ready

**Q1: "How much does it cost? Can I afford this?"**
> Starter: ~$5–15/month for moderate use. Heavy use: $30–50/month. At ₹50K–₹1.5L/month saved in labor, ROI is 50–100x. Frame as investment, not expense. Free tier: none currently, but $5 credit for new accounts.

**Q2: "Is my data safe? Will Anthropic see my company data?"**
> Anthropic doesn't use API data for training (check current policy at anthropic.com/privacy). For highly sensitive data (patient records, legal docs): don't include PII in prompts; anonymize before processing. Enterprise plan has stronger data protection SLAs.

**Q3: "What's the difference between Claude.ai and Claude Code?"**
> Claude.ai = web/app interface, good for one-off tasks. Claude Code = terminal tool, built for developers and automation, can read/write files, run commands, connect to tools (MCPs), spawn agents. This session = Claude Code.

**Q4: "Do I need to know coding to use this?"**
> No. 40% of best use cases require zero coding. You describe outcome in English. Claude writes and runs code. Your job: tell Claude what you want + review outputs. Start with business tasks (content, analysis, data) before touching code.

**Q5: "Can it work with [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com)? We use [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) everywhere."**
> No direct [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) MCP yet. Workaround: Export [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) data (XML or CSV) → Claude processes exported files → generates insights, reports, migration-ready formats. Works well in practice. Advanced: custom [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com) API integration Claude can build.

**Q6: "My business is in Gujarati. Can Claude work in Gujarati?"**
> Yes — Claude reads, writes, translates Gujarati well. Quality: 85-90% vs. English. For critical documents, have Gujarati speaker review Claude output. Tip: write instructions in English, ask Claude to output in Gujarati — better than writing instructions in Gujarati.

**Q7: "Can I use UPI to pay Anthropic?"**
> No. Anthropic accepts international cards only (Visa/Mastercard/Amex). RuPay often doesn't work. Best options: Niyo Global card, Scapia card, HDFC Regalia/Diners — all support international transactions with low/no forex markup.

**Q8: "What if Claude makes a mistake in my accounts/tax?"**
> Claude output = first draft, not final authority. Always have CA/accountant review financial outputs. Use Claude to eliminate 80% of manual work, not 100% of human judgment. Build QA step into workflow: Claude generates → human reviews flagged items only.

**Q9: "Can I build a ChatGPT-like chatbot for my customers using this?"**
> Yes, but Claude Code is for building, not the chatbot interface itself. Claude Code + Anthropic API → build custom chatbot → deploy on website or [WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com). Takes 2–4 hours for basic version. Session demo if time allows — show them the pattern.

**Q10: "How do I convince my boss / team to adopt this?"**
> Don't convince with theory. Build one thing today that solves a real problem they have. Show the output. Let ROI speak. Suggested first wins by role: CA → GST reconciliation demo; Sales → personalized outreach batch; Ops → automated daily report. Demo beats deck every time.

### Watch For During Session
- Attendees who cannot access claude.ai: check they have signed up and are using desktop browser
- API key confusion: many won't have credit card — pair them with someone who does for demo
- Overwhelm at themes breadth: keep anchoring back to "what's YOUR biggest time waster this week?"
- Finance/CA attendees (Theme 3) will have most questions — allocate extra Q&A time
- Non-technical attendees (Theme 9, 10) may feel left behind during dev demos — reassure with non-code examples
- Strong agent interest (Theme 6) from developers — have multi-agent demo ready, this audience goes deep fast
- India-specific tools (GST, [Tally](https://tallysolutions.com), WhatsApp) generate most excitement — lean into these
- [WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com) group: create before session, drop cheatsheet link there — everyone checks [WhatsApp](https://web.whatsapp.com), not email
